Robbery on the Hechao Road Bus: Yesterday, a Hechao bus departed from Fei to Chao. While traveling to Dongshankou, a hundred li from the city, two bandits suddenly produced handguns among the passengers and ordered the driver to stop. Two more bandits emerged from under the bus and boarded, joining in the robbery. None of the passengers were spared. A Mr. Shen had two bowls of opium and 300 silver dollars taken. After obtaining their loot, the bandits alighted and fled.

Correspondence

Letter from Feng Shumin 86

To the Editor,

I recently read a news item in your newspaper's foreign news section titled "Railway Police Department Investigates Case," which is completely contrary to the facts. On June 5th, when the No. 3 express train from Shanghai arrived at Xizhan Station, I was at the station supervising the work. I saw a man in a long gown loitering around, not resembling a passenger. To protect the travelers and prevent any harm, I instructed policeman Zhang Baoyu to pay attention and inquire. Officer Zhang replied that his name was Yang Chunxiang. Officer Zhang believed that I was suspicious because I didn't recognize Yang Chunxiang, so he said the name to avoid further inquiry. However, Yang Chunxiang, with a guilty conscience and feeling apprehensive, thought Zhang's words were unfavorable, so he started to verbally abuse Officer Zhang. Officer Zhang, unwilling to endure the insults, took Yang Chunxiang to the precinct. Even then, Yang Chunxiang pounded the table and chairs, creating a commotion. I moved him to the Public Security Bureau for handling as he was obstructing official duties. This is the factual account of what happened. As for the so-called "Zhang Baoyu fabricating accusations to Police Chief Feng, and Police Chief Feng arresting Yang without careful inquiry," I am not so foolish as to do such a thing. I am writing this letter specifically to request that it be published in the correspondence section, granting a correction to reveal the true facts. Fortunately, the other party has already filed a lawsuit in court, which should resolve the matter according to the law, and the truth will not be difficult to reveal. Respectfully, I wish the editor good health.

Sincerely,

Feng Shumin, Police Chief, Fourth Branch School, Beijing-Shanghai Railway Police

June 16th

Important Education News

Opening of Zhejiang Local Education Administration Conference 87

▲ Opening ceremony held in the morning, chaired by Zhang Nanxian.

▲ Academic lectures and visits to two exhibitions in the afternoon.

The Zhejiang Education Department convened a local education administration conference at 9 a.m. on the 16th in the hall of the department, gathering education directors from various counties and section chiefs from city education bureaus. Attendees included Zhejiang Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Nanxian, Construction Department Director Shi Ying, Zhejiang Provincial Party Department Representative Ye Suzhong, Zhejiang University Representative Yu Ziyi, Education Department Secretary Qian Jiazhi, Hangzhou City Education Section Chief Chen Chengren, and more than fifty education directors from various counties, including Hong Yun. After the ritual led by Chairman Zhang Nanxian, Chairman Zhang delivered an opening speech, stating that holding the local education administration conference today is very important. As Director Zhang is attending the Fifth Plenary Session and has not yet returned to Hangzhou, I have taken the seat on behalf of him. I believe that education and administration are closely related. Those who handle these affairs must identify their goals and go all out. The current social situation is extremely complex. If education fails to get on track or is not handled properly, it could affect the entire situation. Therefore, administrators should take more responsibility and not be negligent. Educational administrators are in a position to guide and supervise. They should have a thorough understanding of the actual situation of various educational aspects and not only consider raising funds as their only capability. When opinions or disagreements arise, they should proactively seek ways to resolve them and eliminate them before they become visible. The quality of education in a province depends on whether the education directors are competent. The current state of education in our country tends toward abnormal development. Rural primary schools are often few in number. I hope that the education directors will pay attention to this point and use propaganda methods to make local people aware of the importance of educating their children, turning negative influences into positive forces to jointly promote educational progress. The implementation of policies should be based on the actual conditions of the local area for more effective results. For example, in rural communities, attention should be paid to agricultural education so that children, after receiving education, have a close relationship with the local area (integrating education with society to achieve the purpose of education as life). How to design and advance local education is what I hope everyone will study together. General meetings often have many proposals. During the meetings, there is much fanfare, but there is no in-depth study. Proposals are rashly passed and the discussion results are printed into booklets and distributed, which is considered done. This kind of self-deception defeats the purpose of the meeting. I hope that everyone attending this meeting will treat the local situation with the attitude of parents, do their best for the local children, and jointly study and discuss it. Then, Qian Jiazhi delivered a speech on behalf of the Education Department Director, followed by speeches by Ye Suzhong, Feng Keshu, Chen Chengren, Shen Baotang, Wang Tianze, Tong Pengchao, Yu Chenghu, Chen Weihan, Sun Ruihuan, and others. The speeches were too long to be recorded in full. The morning session adjourned after 12 o'clock. In the afternoon, at 1:30, an academic lecture was held. The speaker was Zheng Yaocang, and the topic was a general view of primary school education in various schools seen in Shanghai. The lecture lasted about an hour, and the audience was satisfied. After the lecture, everyone identified themselves as members of the group meeting, which was divided into five groups: education administration, education funding, school education, social education, and others. After the identification, the whole group set off to Yunsihe Xiaxue Palace to visit the Hangzhou City Education Equipment Exhibition and the Hang County Common Sense Science Teaching Exhibition.

Zhejiang Education Director Zhang Daofan Rescinds Resignation and Returns to Office 88

Zhejiang Education Director Zhang Daofan previously proposed his resignation due to difficulties in the province's education funding and the difficulty in advancing all plans. The Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Education Department instructed various departments to retain him, as reported in this newspaper. Zhejiang Provincial Chairman Zhang Nanxian visited Zhang Daofan in person while in Beijing to discuss important matters and persuaded him to return to the province. Zhang Daofan agreed to rescind his resignation and originally planned to return to Hangzhou with him. However, due to the Fifth Plenary Session being in progress, Zhang Daofan had to attend the conference and could not accompany him. It is now learned that the Plenary Session has concluded, and Zhang Daofan returned to his office yesterday.

League of Nations Promotes Communication Between Chinese and Western Academics 89

The Ministry of Education previously received a request from the president of National Central University to forward a request to the League of Nations to send professors to China to hold lectures. The ministry forwarded the request to the League of Nations for consideration. Later, a letter was received from League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, stating that the League's Committee on Intellectual Cooperation would carefully consider the methods for promoting academic communication between the League of Nations and China. It is heard that Mr. Wu Zhihui, the representative of China, will be attending the meeting in July, which will further facilitate this matter. Regarding the proposals from China, the Committee on Intellectual Cooperation will review the three points mentioned in the special letter during or around the annual meeting. Preliminary discussions have been made: (1) Regarding the selection of famous professors to give lectures, such as in medicine, natural sciences, and political law, etc., the International Institute of Intellectual Cooperation has been asked to consult with famous universities in Europe. After receiving a report, joint discussions can be held with the Chinese government and the Committee on Intellectual Cooperation of the League of Nations. (2) Regarding the proposal from National Central University to send one professor each for British literature, geography, and geology to the school to hold lectures, the committee is currently consulting with schools and will follow the school's limited nationality of professors and the fixed amount of remuneration indicated in the special letter. (3) Regarding the scope of the League of Nations' cultural movement cooperation projects, such as the work reports of the International Institute of Intellectual Cooperation and the Educational Activities Photography Institute, especially those that can be used as a reference for joint cooperation between China and the League of Nations, the committee has already sent the general outline of the regulations of the Institute to the relevant department. It is hoped that it will be sent to China in the near future. The cultural cooperation organs of the League of Nations expressed their welcome to the proposals from China and showed their support in promoting the cultural progress of China and the League of Nations and in promoting communication between Chinese and Western academics.

Regulations on Superintendents of Schools in Provinces and Cities Promulgated by the Ministry of Education 90

The Ministry of Education promulgated thirteen regulations on superintendents of schools in provinces and cities and issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, as well as the Weihaiwei Management Office: "The regulations on superintendents of schools in provinces and cities have been formulated and submitted to the Executive Yuan for forwarding to the National Government for approval and registration, and have been promulgated and distributed by the Ministry of Education. Please comply with and follow them. Furthermore, from the date of promulgation of these regulations, the Regulations on Superintendents of Schools promulgated by this Ministry in February of the 18th year of the Republic of China are hereby repealed. Please be informed accordingly."

▲ Regulations on Superintendents of Schools in Provinces and Cities

Article 1: Each provincial education department shall have four to eight superintendents of schools, who shall be recommended by the provincial government. Each municipal education bureau under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan shall have two to four superintendents of schools, who shall be recommended or appointed by the municipal government. Under the command of the superior officer, they shall inspect and guide educational matters within their respective jurisdictions.

Article 2: Those with one of the following qualifications may serve as superintendents of schools: (1) Graduates of domestic or foreign university education colleges or liberal arts colleges with an education department who have held educational positions for more than two years and have achieved significant results. (2) Graduates of domestic or foreign specialized schools above the undergraduate level who have held educational positions for more than three years and have achieved significant results. (3) Graduates of senior high school normal departments or normal schools who have held educational positions for more than seven years and have achieved significant results.

Article 3: The matters that superintendents of schools shall inspect and guide are as follows: (1) Matters related to the implementation of education laws and regulations. (2) Matters related to local education administration. (3) Matters related to local education funding. (4) Matters related to school education. (5) Matters related to social education. (6) Matters related to compulsory education. (7) Matters related to the service and performance evaluation of local education personnel. (8) Matters specifically assigned by the superior education administrative officer for inspection or guidance.

Article 4: In addition to regular inspections, superintendents of schools may be dispatched by the superior education administrative officer for temporary inspections in the event of special circumstances.

Article 5: Before departing for a regular inspection, the superintendent of schools shall formulate forms based on the standards stipulated in Article 3 and submit them to the superior education administrative officer for approval.

Article 6: When inspecting various schools and other educational institutions, the superintendent of schools may review various books and records.

Article 7: The superintendent of schools may inspect the number of students and test their academic performance at any time.

Article 8: The superintendent of schools may temporarily change the school's class schedule when necessary to perform their duties.

Article 9: The superintendent of schools shall correct any violations of laws and regulations at any time during inspections.

Article 10: The superintendent of schools may convene local education personnel at any location to solicit opinions and discuss methods of implementation.

Article 11: The superintendent of schools may stay in educational institutions or public places during inspections, but may not accept their supplies.

Article 12: The superintendent of schools shall report in detail to the superior education administrative officer on the matters inspected and guided in Article 3. The superior education administrative officer shall summarize and forward the reports to the Ministry of Education.

Article 13: The superintendent of schools shall not concurrently hold positions in schools or other institutions.

Article 14: The inspection area and duration of the superintendent of schools and the distribution of their tasks shall be determined and implemented by the superior education administrative officer.

Article 15: The detailed rules of procedure, salary, and travel expenses of the superintendent of schools shall be determined by the superior education administrative officer and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 16: The superior education administrative officer of each province and city may hire specialized inspectors when necessary. The provisions of Articles 6 to 12 shall apply to specialized inspectors.

Article 17: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Jia Ding Infant Health Competition 91

The Jia Ding County Kui Shan District Public Education Center held the second Infant Health Competition on June 14th, along with a health education exhibition. County Magistrate Chen and Education Director Yang chaired the meeting at 8:00 am, and the examinations began at 9:00 am. Famous Shanghai doctors Heng Zhuoren, Wang Yugang, Huang Yexiong, Zhang Jinchi, Cheng Zhihe, and the director of the center's public treatment center and special appointed doctors were responsible for judging. A total of 154 infants participated, divided into nine stages from six months to sixty months, with six months as one stage. Three winners were selected from each stage. The results were Zhuang Yongsi, Yang Dazong, Lu Xichen, Zhou Weiyi, Zhan Tong, Liang Jinfen, Huang Quanbao, and 27 others who won prizes. Prior to the event, the center entrusted Yang Weiyu and Pan Yangyao of the China Vocational Education Society to solicit prizes. The Shanghai Sanyou Industrial Company, Family Industrial Company, Commercial Press, China Book Company, and Yixin Toothbrush Factory generously donated many prizes. A total of about 2,800 prizes were received. The winners returned with full loads, and even those who did not win prizes were given eight daily necessities.

Everyone dispersed happily. On the same day, the center also prepared a self-made animated picture box, depicting various infant care situations, titled "Min'er's Mother".

At the same time, the "Min'er's Mother" from the China Vocational Education Society was distributed.

The audience read and watched the small vocational booklet with great interest.

Amendments to the City's 94

Primary School Teacher Qualification and Registration Regulations 95

The Shanghai Education Bureau yesterday announced the revised regulations for the examination and registration of primary school teachers. It convened schools in the city and said, "The regulations for the examination and the registration of primary school teachers in this city have been slightly revised, and the points reviewed and revised in the Municipal Government's Order No. 10552 are still feasible and should be approved for record. Please comply with and implement them." Therefore, it should be announced and implemented. The copy of the revised regulations is as follows:

▲ Regulations of Shanghai Education Bureau for Examining Primary School Teachers (Revised and promulgated by Shanghai Special Municipal Government in December of the 18th year of the Republic of China, and re-revised on June 10th of the 20th year of the Republic of China). Article 1: These regulations are formulated based on Item 5 of Clause B of Article 4 of the Organizational Rules of the Shanghai Education Bureau. Article 2: All examinations of primary school teachers in this city shall be handled in accordance with these regulations. Article 3: Anyone who has passed the registration review of the current primary school teachers is allowed to be exempt from the examination. Article 4: Anyone

who has one of the following qualifications and wishes to serve as a teacher in a primary school in this city shall be subject to examination: 1. Graduates of a normal elementary course or a training course of one year. 2. Graduates of a junior high school. 3. Those who have studied at a secondary school for more than three years. 4. Those who have been primary school teachers for more than three consecutive years. 5. Those who have passed the examination but have lost their validity. 6. Graduates of senior high schools and old-system middle schools who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years. 7. Graduates of vocational schools (with the same level as senior high schools) or old-system Class A industrial schools who have worked in institutions unrelated to their major for more than two years. 8. Graduates of rural normal schools or normal training courses with a study period of three years or less but more than two years who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years. 9. Graduates of nursery training institutes or nursery departments with a study period of two years or more who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years. 10. Graduates of unregistered private secondary schools who have served as teachers in national, provincial, municipal, county-level, or registered private schools for more than one year without registration. 11. Those who have studied specialized academics and have achieved considerable results. Article 5: Those who are examined shall register with the Bureau and submit two recent 2.5-inch half-length photos, along with graduation certificates, study certificates, examination certificates, service certificates, etc., for verification and complete various forms. "Those who are examined may request a list of educational books and practice questions that primary school teachers should study at the registration office." The various certificates mentioned above shall only be returned after the examination is completed. Article 6: The registration and examination dates and locations shall be announced by the Bureau in the newspaper. Article 7: The examination is divided into three items: physical examination, written examination, and oral examination. Those who fail the physical examination are not allowed to take the written or oral examinations. Article 8: The subjects of the written examination are divided into two types: class teachers and specialized teachers. A. The subjects of the written examination for class teachers are (1) Party Principles, (2) Chinese Language, (3) Arithmetic, (4) General Knowledge, (5) Education. B. The subjects of the written examination for specialized teachers are (1) Party Principles, (2) Chinese Language, (3) General Knowledge, (4) Education, (5) Specialized Subject. Article 9: Those who pass the examination shall be issued an examination certificate by the Bureau. Article 10: The valid period of the examination certificate is three years. Article 11: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. Article 12: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

▲ Regulations of Shanghai Education Bureau for Registering Primary School Teachers (Approved and promulgated by the Municipal Government on December 11th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, and revised and promulgated on June 10th of the 20th year of the Republic of China). Article 1: Primary school teachers in this city shall register with the Bureau in accordance with these regulations. Article 2: Anyone who has one of the following qualifications from national, provincial, municipal, county-level, or registered private schools shall be allowed to register after passing the oral examination and physical examination: 1. Graduates of university education departments, education colleges, or normal universities. 2. Graduates of university undergraduate (excluding education departments), advanced normal schools, or advanced normal specialized courses. 3. Graduates of specialized schools (excluding advanced normal schools). 4. Graduates of senior high school normal departments or normal undergraduate courses. 5. Graduates of rural normal schools with a study period of four years or more. 6. Graduates of senior high schools or old-system middle schools, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation. 7. Graduates of vocational schools (with the same level as senior high schools) or old-system Class A industrial schools, but this does not apply to those who have worked in institutions related to their major for more than two years after graduation. 8. Graduates of rural normal schools or normal training courses with a study period of three years or less but more than two years, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation. 9. Graduates of nursery training institutes or nursery departments with a study period of two years or more, but this does not apply to those who have worked in non-educational institutions for more than two years after graduation. Article 3: Those who have passed the examination and have not exceeded the prescribed time limit are allowed to register. The valid time of registration is the same as the valid time of the examination. Article 4: Teachers who are allowed to register and meet the qualifications in the first, second, fourth, fifth, sixth, and eighth items of the preceding article are allowed to serve as class teachers. Those who meet the qualifications in the third and seventh items are allowed to serve as specialized teachers. Those who meet the qualifications in the ninth item are allowed to serve as nannies. Those who meet the qualifications in the third article are allowed to serve in the positions for which they have passed the examination. Article 5: The registration of teachers who have been approved for registration and continue to work in non-educational institutions or institutions unrelated to their major for more than two years is invalid. Article 6: Two registration forms for primary school teachers must be completed at the time of registration, each with a recent 2.5-inch half-length photo. Article 7: Graduation certificates, examination certificates, service certificates, etc. must be submitted for verification at the time of registration and will be returned after the registration results are announced. Article 8: One registration form will be returned to those who are allowed to register. Registration forms will not be returned to those who fail. Article 9: The registration date of each session will be announced by the Bureau in the newspaper. Article 10: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. Article 11: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

County Education Bureau Reprimands He Po Elementary School and 22 Other Schools 96

▲ For not submitting exhibits to the Arithmetic Teaching Aids Exhibition

The Shanghai County Education Bureau yesterday issued an order reprimanding He Po Elementary School and 22 other schools, stating that the Bureau organized the Arithmetic Teaching Aids Exhibition to improve arithmetic teaching in various schools and increase children's interest in learning. It was included in the Bureau's 19th year policy plan, and the methods had already been notified. The number of exhibits was not strictly limited, and subsidies were provided for the production of the products. All were recorded and checked in advance. The Chao Shang Ju Maritime College Might Be Shut Down 97

Since the China Merchants Bureau was reorganized by the National Government, Zhao Tieqiao, the former director-general, established a nautical science college at the original China Merchants Public School in Tilanqiao to cultivate nautical talents and develop China's shipping industry. The first graduating class was employed on ships, and the second graduating class will soon be on board for practical training this term. Last year, during the tenure of Commissioner Li Zhonggong, the bureau was nationalized and should have been further developed for domestic shipping affairs and the cultivation of specialized nautical talents. Last winter, the educational departments of various provinces were separately sent letters to continue recruiting 180 preparatory students, divided into three departments: navigation, marine engineering, and business. The specialized school was renamed the State-Operated China Merchants Bureau Maritime College. This year, the preparatory students will graduate and enter the undergraduate program during the summer vacation. Guo Waifeng, the newly appointed commissioner, intends to announce the closure of the school due to the bureau's financial constraints. Upon hearing this news, the students of the school panicked and elected representatives to visit Commissioner Guo to request that he withdraw the decision and continue operating the school. However, no satisfactory results were obtained. It is reported that they will organize a school protection movement, submit a petition to the National Government, issue a declaration, and request assistance from all parties.

World News in Brief 105

— Hai Ke

▲ Due to the census to be held in England and Wales in 1931, they are rushing to produce a very large map two years in advance. All the main roads and small alleys in the country are included. This is the most detailed map ever made.

▲ A proposal has been made in the German Parliament to give preferential treatment to servants employed by families. They must have nine hours of sleep and four hours of vacation every day, and officials will be sent to inspect their food and bedding. If this proposal is passed, it will become law.

▲ In 1929, Britain built a new ocean liner for the East called "Orentes". The promenade deck is particularly large, allowing passengers to enjoy three-quarters of a mile of walking. There is also an outdoor swimming pool for swimming.

▲ Within the Gold Coast region of Africa, there are several very good native schools that provide natives with considerable education. Also, Accra, an important town in the Crown Colony, has a well-equipped hospital, which is unprecedented in the wilderness.

▲ Women in American high society like to raise dogs as a fashionable gesture. As a result, many young ladies are going to work as maids in kennels, serving their mistresses' beloved dogs just as they serve their sons and daughters.

A Record of the Memorial Service for General Lu Shidi 106

— Sun Choucheng

It has been almost half a year since the death of General Lu Xiqing. Comrades in Shanghai, remembering their old friendship, held a memorial service at the Buddhist Jingye Society on Hedder Road on the 14th of this month to express their condolences. Here is what I saw and heard, recorded and sent to Free Talk, to inform all comrades who did not attend that day.

I went at 1 p.m. that day. After getting out of the car, the tall, cloud-piercing white archway at the entrance came into view. A horizontal plaque hung on it, reading "Memorial Service for General Lu Xiqing of the Army." Next to it was a red satin inscription presented by Commander-in-Chief Chiang, about ten feet high, adorned with a colorful pavilion. After entering and signing in, each person was given a piece of black gauze and a white paper flower. There were hundreds of memorial banners and elegiac couplets hanging on both sides. Here are some that I remember: Mayor Zhang sent a scroll with a five-character ancient poem, which read: "At seven years old, his reputation grew. In his prime, he showed outstanding achievements. His heart was filled with the idea of serving the country. He was a model for our Party. Who would have thought that he was ill in bed, and suddenly he passed away. Alas, you died young. How hasty your departure was! The wind and clouds are tragic, and the sun is setting in the west. A strong hawk soared into the sky, but broke its heaven-reaching wings. A huge fish migrated from the sea, but lost its strength in the middle of the journey. Sad cries come from the sea, and the hub of power turns pale. Posthumous awards honor past glory, and posthumous honors show final adornments. Relatives and friends share the same grief, and the streets and alleys are filled with sorrow. My friendship with you was especially deep, and my sadness is truly endless. We gather together to summon your soul, and my tears flow freely as I write." Commander Xiong's elegy read: "The cuckoo cries for five nights, sadly seeing the great star destroy the general." "Half a lifetime in the saddle, the history books should record his great achievements." The entrance to the auditorium was decorated with white ribbons, and a horizontal plaque with the four characters "Model Party Member" hung above it, presented by 72 Party members from Sichuan, including Wang Xujiu and Lv Dan'ai. Inside the room, a white satin embroidered curtain hung high, with a portrait of General Lu in the center, smiling kindly, without any military air. On the sacrificial table were sixteen tall basins filled with tea, snacks, and fruits, as well as a vegetarian feast and two vases of fresh flowers. The walls were covered with elegiac couplets from Chiang Kai-shek, Hu Hanmin, Yu Youren, and Xie Chi, all lamenting his extraordinary talent and revolutionary ideas, and regretting his early death, which was a misfortune for the Party and the country. Dozens of wreaths were piled up on the ground, looking like a flower mound from a distance. Kneeling to the left of the stage were the filial sons, only four or five years old. General Lu's sisters, Ms. Han Shu and his younger brother, Shi Zhuan, all wore white clothes and Buddhist beads around their necks, with sorrowful expressions on their faces. Chairman Chiang originally planned to attend the memorial service in person, but he was going to Jiangxi to suppress the bandits and was preparing to leave soon, so he could not spare the time. Therefore, he sent Yang Hu, a military attaché of the National Government, as his representative. During the ceremony, he first offered flowers, then fruit, and finally food, and then read the eulogy. The text was very sad, with phrases such as "Alas, the jade is broken and the orchid is withered, the country is devastated, and the excellence remains immortal, the coffin is hidden in the ground." General Lu was loyal and upright, with profound knowledge and foresight. He dedicated himself to the revolution in the late Qing Dynasty and followed the Premier for more than ten years, rushing about for national affairs and enduring hardships. When Chen Jiongming betrayed the Premier, General Lu united his troops and recovered Guangzhou, a great achievement. To sum up his life, he devoted himself to the Party and the country, and remained loyal to his principles from beginning to end. Even in his illness, he did not forget national affairs and often wrote thousands of words to Chairman Chiang, silently supporting military strategies and harmonizing Party views. When he was seriously ill and lacked medical expenses, his comrades raised funds to help him, which shows his integrity throughout his life. His name was Lu Shidi, and his courtesy name was Xiqing. He was from Chengdu, Sichuan. He served as the commander of the Third Army directly under the Central Government, a senator in the Military Advisory Council, and a member of the Sichuan Provincial Government. He died at the age of only forty-five. Therefore, when his life was briefly reported that day, all the comrades present sighed that a wise man had withered. I returned and wrote this to express my condolences.

An Elopement by Airplane 108

— Mou Keque

When two people are in love but are constrained by their circumstances and cannot marry openly, elopement is the last resort. However, this is only when both parties are passionately in love and do not consider that one day the truth will come out. Elopement values speed, which is inevitable. Today, science is flourishing, and the sailboats and horse-drawn carriages of the past are gradually becoming outdated and are being replaced by steam engines. Since the invention of airplanes that can soar in the sky, the speed of steam engines pales in comparison. Therefore, postal workers and travelers are relying on airplanes for speed. Everything is modernizing, so why can't elopement be fashionable? However, since the beginning of aviation in our country, no one has ever eloped by airplane. The following story is truly a new record for elopement. If Hong Fu knew about it in the afterlife, she would be ashamed of herself.

To the east of Songjiang is Sijing Town. The town is densely populated and is the leading town in Songjiang Prefecture. Gu Yushang was born there. He graduated from a law school and is now a trainee judge at the Shanghai District Court. His wife, Fei Guoying, is from Xinqiao Town, twelve miles from Sijing. She is beautiful and wealthy. Since their marriage,

their relationship has been quite close. However, three years ago, Gu met a woman named Zhong and took her as a concubine. Since then, conflicts arose between the wife and the concubine, and Zhong soon passed away. Gu had previously been a trial judge in Qidong County. This spring, he was transferred to Changshu. At that time, a clerk named Gui Jianhong was also a clerk in Changshu. Gu and his wife stayed in the county government office, and Gui entered their rooms freely. Fei and Gu's love affair began. At first, Gu did not know, so the secret affair continued. Before long, Gu was transferred to the Shanghai District Court and took his family with him. The pair of lovebirds were separated. However, the more love is suppressed, the more it grows. To suddenly stop it would cause a backlash. Fei asked her husband to go to Yu to study, but she actually stayed with Gui in the Daxin Hotel on Qianjie Street in Changshu. Her husband found out and they fled to Shanghai together. One day, Gu met them at the Jiangsu Hotel and questioned them severely, revealing the secret. The next day, he took her back to Sijing and beat her severely, causing her serious injuries. He then locked her in a room, cutting her off from the world. Her paternal aunt, who was over sixty years old, found out and secretly released her. Fei took her jewelry and went to the Hongqiao Airport in Shanghai, where she boarded a plane and flew away. She went from Beijing to Wuxi, and from Wuxi to Yu, hoping to be with her lover for the rest of her life. Her husband tracked her down, but she had already disappeared. It is now said that Fei has been arrested in Songjiang, and Gu has filed a lawsuit in the local court and is about to go to court. The storm in the sea of love is just beginning.

Discussing the Efficacy of Stinky Water in Preventing Epidemics 109

— Wulu

The air is dry in the summer, and germs spread very quickly. If preventive measures are not taken early, epidemics will arise and cause future troubles.

The harm is truly not insignificant.

In Shanghai, no fewer than several thousand people die each year due to epidemics in the summer. The reason for this is that people do not know how to prevent them. Therefore, knowledgeable people should pay attention to summer hygiene and purchase antiseptic solution as soon as possible to eliminate the foul air and eradicate infectious germs in the air. This will allow them to rest easy. Antiseptic stinky water contains a large amount of carbolic acid. If it is used to sprinkle indoors, in kitchens, on ditches, in wall corners, in latrines, in chamber pots, and in dirty places, mosquitoes, flies, and germs will be eradicated, and toxins will have no way to spread. Therefore, stinky water is of great help to summer epidemic prevention work. However, the annual demand is very large, and purchasing foreign goods results in the loss of rights. I have heard that the Yalin antiseptic stinky water produced by the Wuzhou Pharmacy's own factory has very complete manufacturing equipment and is made with German equipment, so the products are excellent and reliable. I would like to introduce it to readers, because in the name of epidemic prevention, I am also promoting domestic goods.

The volume is prefaced by prefaces from famous figures Hu Boxiang and Zhu Shourentian, and inscriptions from Zhu Yingpeng, Zhang Zhenhou, Lang Jingshan, Li Denghui, Hu Bozhou, and Chen Qiucao, which makes it even more valuable. The content is rich, with as many as sixty-six fine art works. The editors are Zhao Yun, Zhang Mingguang, Cao Zuguang, and Xu , from the Society. Xu Huijun, a graduate of the University, and Chen Bingde, the director of physical education, strongly supported it, so its results can be regarded as representative photographic works of the student era. (Kuan)

Cultural Movements the Capital Should Undertake in the Future (Part 2) 110

— Wang Yachen

The holding of this Capital Art Exhibition has given people a very good impression. In the future, I hope that the educational and administrative organs of the capital and all those who are concerned about cultural undertakings will pay attention to art museums, which are even more necessary than exhibitions, and promote their realization. Exhibitions are temporary and are essential to promoting modern art. Art museums are permanent and are essential to promoting and preserving the spirit of our country's past art. Furthermore, the main purpose of art museums has the following two points.

(1) Enhance the Status of Contemporary Art: Our country's art, whether it is painting, sculpture, music, craftsmanship, etc., has been brilliant in history and has a considerable status in itself. Even other countries praise China's past art in unison. However, in modern times, it has declined. The reason for this decline is that recent writers lack in-depth research, especially during the research period, there is a lack of deep knowledge of the techniques of the ancients. In the past, domestic collectors were unwilling to show their masterpieces to others easily. Therefore, it was very difficult for researchers to obtain references. Because of the lack of references, their understanding was not profound. If their understanding is not profound, they will produce crude and shoddy works. Therefore, Chinese art is gradually declining. Art researchers in various countries, when exploring techniques, all linger in art museums, learning from ancient research to produce emerging art of the times. This is a necessary process. By reviewing the old, we know the new, and creation is also based on this. With the lure of the ancients in history, there will be progress for future generations. No one will be born a creator. They must know the path of learning from good temptations and enter the palace of art through the path of learning. The establishment of art museums not only preserves the authority of inherent art, but also enhances the status of contemporary art.

(2) Expand the Status of International Art: Art is the flag of culture and the darling of the times. If art is not vibrant, culture will decline. Whether or not a country's art progresses depends entirely on the direction of the art of the times. When foreigners set foot on our land and see the facilities of art museums, they can ponder in them. This is most likely to give travelers a good impression. International art promotion is indeed based on this. To compete for international status, although it contains various facilities, the organization of art and its promotion to the outside world is truly powerful. In recent years, the Japanese have been promoting Eastern culture to Europe at the cost of huge sums of money, sparing no effort. People of all countries have considerable sympathy for the Japanese. Looking back at our country, we are lagging behind and are overshadowed by the Japanese. According to Japanese art, it originated in our country. Therefore, today we must have considerable publicity internationally. The first step in promoting art internationally is to organize our own works of art. Organizing the inherent essence and establishing an art museum is an urgent matter.

Rotary Club Lecture

Three Eras (9) 111

— Zhang Henshui

(4) The Athlete's Revenge

From that day on, Zhang Xiaosan became a soldier. After becoming a soldier, he realized that it was not as comfortable as he had imagined. Just learning how to march, he was beaten twenty or thirty times. When he was a rickshaw puller, he could run or argue back when the police beat him. Now, the platoon leaders and squad leaders who taught him drills slapped him so hard that he wasn't even allowed to move. The filial piety of sons to their fathers in the world can never be that reverent. What was it for? For six big dollars a month in salary. This six dollars was originally calculated by discounting ten dollars. But now, even the discounted amount cannot be paid. Zhang Xiaosan had been a soldier for four months and had only received two dollars. He used to earn that much pulling a rickshaw in a single day. However, riding the streetcar for free, listening to operas for free, and going to brothels for free were all facts. He had tried them all several times. This day was a beautiful day with clear autumn skies. The military camp had a half-day holiday. The platoon leader took them out of the city to visit the Sanbeizi Garden for free. When they returned, everyone rode the streetcar for free, heading straight from Xizhimen to Qianmen. But when the streetcar reached the Nongshangbu Street intersection, it broke down. It suddenly stopped. Those who had paid to ride the streetcar had to accept their bad luck. These young gentlemen were a little impatient. Two of them had already opened the window and leaned out to look. They saw a large crowd gathered in the middle of the street. According to the onlookers, four or five rickshaw pullers were fighting each other. It was going to be a matter of life and death. When the soldiers heard this, they thought, "It's no wonder the streetcar driver didn't want to drive." Everyone got off the streetcar and went forward to watch. They saw three policemen squeezing into the crowd of fighting people, shouting, "Stop fighting! Stop fighting! Everyone go to the police station!" As they spoke, they struck the entangled fighters with their batons. A soldier cursed, "Damn, the black dogs are unreasonable. Why are they hitting people too?" Zhang Xiaosan remembered being beaten with a police baton on Nongshangbu Street in the past. Immediately, sparks flew in his heart. His eyes widened, and he cursed, "Damn it! They always make trouble for rickshaw pullers. Good boy! You try moving me now! I'll beat you until you eat shit!" The policemen maintaining order and the soldiers defending the country were each doing their own duty. No one would have thought that there would be any hatred. Moreover, the policemen and soldiers both belonged to the armed class.

Japanese merchants are purchasing, and at the same time, yarn prices are rising sharply, making the situation even tighter. Prices are up 6 or 7 qian for various months.

▲Hankou Standard: Large Traders Cover Short Positions In the early market, the Hankou standard cotton price rose by 3 or 4 qian, excluding outside cotton. In the afternoon, with the yarn market soaring and large traders covering short positions, prices rose another 3 qian for various months. Total transactions for the day were 87,600 dan. Chang Ji sold 1,800 dan, Yi Yu 2,000 dan, Yong Chang 2,500 dan, and Yi Cheng 2,400 dan. Da Feng bought 2,100 dan, Tian Long 7,700 dan, Chang Feng 2,600 dan, and Zhen Da 2,800 dan.

Yuan Da bought 2,800 dan. The closing prices are recorded on the left.

Hankou Standard Closing Prices: Month Close Change Balance August 39.95 Up 8.0 56,000 June 39.71 Up 6.0 83,100 October 38.25 Up 7.0 156,500 July 40.00 Up 8.0 154,400 November 37.95 Up 6.0 105,400 ▲Rumors of Outer Factories Importing Shaanxi Cotton: Spot cotton trading is very quiet. The source of supply includes 300 pieces of Mu Jia cotton and 68 bales of Yao cotton. There are rumors that Jardine Matheson is importing 2,500 pieces of Shaanxi cotton, but this has yet to be confirmed.

Foreign Yarn and Cotton Rise Unanimously 118

▲American Cotton Rebounds After Dipping: Yesterday, the American cotton market was calm. At the closing, due to buying by fellow traders and short covering, the price suddenly rose. Futures rose by 26 to 27 points, and spot prices rose by 30 points.

British cotton futures rose by 4 points, and spot prices rose by 1 point. Egyptian cotton spot prices rose by 5 points. Indian cotton was very firm due to short covering and hedging. Pingguoer and Aomula rose by 4 rupees, and Bailuoxi rose by 5 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (dated the 16th):

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Factory Silk Quotes Rise

Yesterday, the local foreign firm silk market gradually showed a firm rise, due to rising silk prices in overseas markets. Shanghai white factory silk gradually saw a turnaround in Shanghai, and European firms actively covered their short positions. As factory costs were heavy, they insisted on selling only at higher prices. Yesterday, it was estimated that Lien and others imported 50 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, with prices rising sharply by 5 taels.

Current State of Summer Silkworms in Chang'an is Still Good 119

Due to the poor spring cocoon harvest this year, silkworm farmers in the Chang'an area of Zhejiang province have suffered losses. Many have started to raise summer silkworms to compensate. The silkworm eggs are strong. After hatching, the weather has been sunny and warm, and the conditions have been good. The early batch has already completed its third molt and started eating leaves. The earlier rainstorm had some ill effects on the silkworms. The later batches of silkworms are still young, with little impact. Instructors are currently trying to remedy the situation. Fortunately, the weather cleared up yesterday, and the current state is still good.

Lu Zhuang's Fine Eyebrow Tea Sees Slight Movement in European Sales 120

Yesterday, in the local foreign firm tea market, the fine eyebrow green tea from Wudong and Tunxi in the Lu Zhuang area began to be searched for again due to telegram inquiries received last week. However, merchants' price requests remained harsh, and sales were not widespread. The situation is still difficult to consider good. Although the needle eyebrow and bud eyebrow teas have seen slight activity, the market has also failed to improve. Gao Zhuang's Gongxi and Baitou Zhuang's Fulin

and Qianyi firms have all made purchases. However, the Russian Aid Association, which has a large sales network,

has not yet completed the procedures for last year's purchases of Gongxi tea.

Discussions about opening new goods are currently difficult to make. This point is a very important key to the future of green tea.

Piece Goods: Fine Twill Suddenly Surges: Local Cotton Cloth: Sanpin surges, market sentiment is firm and rising, with fine twill being the strongest, showing a tendency to soar. The reason is that the Guangdong groups are actively purchasing, and it is also cheaper than fine cloth. Speculators are all seeking to hoard it, and the price has risen uniformly by a significant amount. Yanghe is selling for 7 taels 6 qian 2 fen and 5 li, and Blue Double Fish is 7 taels 5 qian 2 fen and 5 li.

Squirrel is 7 taels and 5 fen. Fine cloth is increasingly scarce. Trumpet Boy and Colored Ball have already been cleared at 7 taels and 7 qian. Blue Chicken is 7 taels and 5 qian 5 fen, and Blue Flying Fish is 8 taels and 5 fen. However, coarse twill is not only not rising, but Three Fish, Three Rabbit, and Cat and Eagle are all lackluster, due to the quiet sales channels.

▲East and West Piece Goods: Market conditions are increasingly trending upward. The Yuan Yu silk,

Bamboo Forest Qingguan Mirror of eastern goods have all reached 12 taels 2 qian and 5 fen. Fine serge is also gradually rising. Huxinting is 3 qian 4 fen and 7 li and 5 hao, Sanyou Tu is 3 qian 3 fen and 7 li and 5 hao. Gongsun Tu of lower garment goods has also been cleared at 3 qian and 1 fen. Sales to Sichuan groups remain smooth. Changsha groups replenished a large batch yesterday, but the attitude of the Tianjin group is slightly calmer, as they have already been hoarding in Osaka. This is why the Sanpin price suddenly rose yesterday. The demand for Yuehua velvet by the Sichuan group is very strong, with over 500 pieces traded yesterday. Medium stem is 2 qian 4 fen and 7 li and 5 hao, and large stem is 2 qian and 5 fen and 5 hao. Black flower is out of stock. Yuan Yu silk, Tai Xi satin, and Ruler Six Yuan velvet of western goods are all scarce, and there is a risk of future stockouts.

Grain: He Xia Rice Market is Gradually Firm

▲Xin Zha: Yesterday, the rice market felt increasingly flat, and buying sentiment was difficult to boost. The opening price in the morning had limited fluctuations. Changxi premium goods were slightly loose, and Bo Dao Shang Zhan was unusually quiet. The overall market fell again. Although the inventory of early rice was scarce, the situation was reversed and prices were low.

The demand for glutinous rice was slightly better, but the market was unstable. Du Jian sales were still good, and prices remained firm. Very few people were at the Yangbu Jian market in the morning. Yangmi xiangcang groups still traded well, but local street buying was limited, and prices did not rise or fall. Ships arriving from the west included seventeen or eighteen vessels from Changshu, Wuxi, Liyang, Jiangyin, Kunshan, Jiaoli, and Chonggu.

▲Hu Nan: Yesterday, 14 or 15 ships arrived at the rice market from various groups inland.

The transportation of thick Japonica rice from Changxi was heavy, and it was slightly more active at the end. Qingpu and Fengjing's thin rice stores continued to rise. Su Chang and Beigeng were unattended, and prices fell by 5 fen. The sales of Dao Du and Yang Jian were normal, and there was no original or unadulterated product on the market. The flow of Yin Hua goods was high, and prices were low.

Sugar Market: Coarse Granulated White Sugar Continues to Open for Over a Thousand Bags

▲Daily Sugar Allocation Market Slightly

Yesterday, the sugar market production area telegram reported that the price of spot Cuban sugar had not changed. The price of New York sugar futures for September was up two points compared to the previous telegram, and the price of each other month rose by one point.

The price of spot and future Javan sugar remains stable. Market allocation for public associations remained flat,

and buying sentiment was sluggish. Dutch No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar was priced at 11 taels and 7 qian, but there were very few takers. No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was priced at 11 taels and 5 fen, but transactions were also scarce. Dutch red sugar No. 12 rose to 10 taels and 1 qian, still at a fair price. Japanese sugar import and export was also slack, demand was even quieter, and the market also fell slightly. M Mark was 11 taels 3 qian and 2.5 fen, SH Mark was 11 taels 1 qian and 2.5 fen, YP Mark was 11 taels and 7 qian, YT Mark was 11 taels 3 qian, YRO Mark was 10 taels and 9 qian 7.5 fen, AE Mark was 11 taels and 7 qian 2.5 fen to 7 qian, Taikoo DY Mark was 11 taels and 2 qian, and the trend was still rising. Transaction volume was slow.

Hwa Sing sold more than one thousand bags of spot coarse granulated white sugar at 11 taels and 7 qian, and the market was stable and unremarkable.

North-South Goods: Hao Red Dates Open for Over a Thousand Packages

▲The Price is 6 Taels and 5 Qian to 7 Qian

Recently, a large amount of Haozhou red dates has arrived, and the shops have opened sales for the past two days. A total of over a thousand packages have been traded, with prices ranging from 6 taels and 7 qian to 5 qian.

Each shop has distributed the orders. The previous market had slightly increased in color.

As for sales, groups such as Guangdong and Wenzhou are purchasing, and the shop's market price has been sold at over 6 taels and 8 qian.

The market is expected to tighten.
